         1-       -*-mcnpgen-*- 2000MWth MCFR with LME 60cm 12m3 w/ eq. TRU burnup 600 days,n+p   
         2-       c mcnp6 i=mcfr175.txt o=mcfrout175.txt runtpe=mcfrtpe175.txt                    
         3-       c                                                                               
         4-       c Notes aboue input file:                                                       
         5-       c This is file is meant to test to see if input masses are being computed       
         6-       c correctly after being modified in Excel. Full calculation method.             
         7-       c                                                                               
         8-       c This input file evaluates a 12m^3 volume core with a fuel mixture of          
         9-       c 46.15 NaCl - 46 UCl3 - 8.85(TRU)Cl3. The TRU composition used was             
        10-       c provided in the REBUS-3700 design concept. The above fuel composition         
        11-       c was chosen to increase the amount of U-238 in the fuel and keep the           
        12-       c melting point below 650 C.                                                    
        13-       c                                                                               
        14-       c This is the initial code for beginning a burnup calculation which will        
        15-       c take into account fission product removal and additional U-238 being          
        16-       c added to the reactor. Once this first 100 day burnup is complete a new        
        17-       c input file is created and the compostion of the fuel is adjusted so that      
        18-       c an additional burnup run can be performed.                                    
        19-       c                                                                               
        20-       c The geometry of the core is simply a cylinder core with a TZM vessel and      
        21-       c a 60 cm thick lead-magnesium eutectic (LME) reflector outside of the core.    
        22-       c A B4C poison was added beyond the reflector to act a shield and also reduce   
        23-       c the chance of criticality in the heat exchanger.                              
        24-       c                                                                               
        25-       c                                                                               
        26-       c     cell cards                                                                
        27-       c   mat density  Bounding Surfaces importance  temperature                      
        28-       c             Fuel Salts (Core)
